AWGP BOOK CATALOG — ORGANIZED BY TOPIC

LINK FORMAT (per book):
  Buy:          https://www.awgpstore.com/product?id=<BOOK_CODE>
  Read Online:  https://www.awgp.org/en/literature/book/<Book_Name_With_Underscores>/v1

NOTES:
  - Buy links are RELIABLE — they follow AWGP Store's confirmed id-based URL pattern.
  - Read Online links are BEST-EFFORT GUESSES generated by title-casing the catalog's
    book name and joining words with underscores (the only pattern confirmed by example:
    SA12 'ASAN AUR PRANAYAM' -> 'Aasan_Aur_Pranayam'). The catalog name and the live
    awgp.org slug do not always match exactly (spelling/transliteration differences),
    so please SPOT-CHECK each Read Online link before publishing it on the website —
    if a link 404s, search the book title directly on https://www.awgp.org/en/literature
  - Each topic may list multiple related books; pick whichever best fits your page.
  - Language is noted for every title since most of the catalog is in Hindi/regional
    languages — prefer English titles where available for an English-first website.
